     <p> A frozen waterfall is the only way to march south-east from here and will require climbing or rappelling to cross it. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('n0qlCqRx');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Music drifts between two snowy giant boulders.  A warm, honeyed melody inviting you to listen a while. Following the music to its source you find Arntrude, a terrified bard surrounded by sleeping monsters (from the random encounters table). She stares at you in desperation, trapped by her own lullaby and unable to escape. <p> <strong>Arntrude of Ashamar</strong>.       <p> The Swords Of Justice militia are conspiring to overthrow the ruler of the realm. </p>  <p> The militias usual gathering venue is <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/Fw0E6HFn"><strong>"The Bleeding Pixie Tavern"</strong></a> in <strong>Heartseeker Forest</strong> </p> 
      <p> The militia leader is a <strong>Caloanna of Palemoon</strong>, a level 6 Dwarf Fighter.  She has heavy makeup, crystal blue eyes and chubby cheeks (<em>Distressed</em>).    Caloanna has a special interest of an unknown nature in <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/tgN97l5c/npc/sl6mtOjr"><strong>Walo of Dorith</strong></a> .  </p> <strong>Caloanna of Palemoon</strong>
